<s> an unsuccessful campaign of pacification followed over the next two decades during which an estimated 100,000 to 250,000 individuals lost their lives <\s>
<s> on 30 august 1999 in a un-supervised popular referendum an overwhelming majority of the people of timor-leste voted for independence from indonesia <\s>
<s> between the referendum and the arrival of a multinational peacekeeping force in late september 1999 anti-independence timorese militias organized and supported by the indonesian military commenced a large-scale scorched-earth campaign of retribution <\s>
<s> the militias killed approximately 1,400 timorese and forcibly pushed 300,000 people into western timor as refugees <\s>
<s> the majority of the country's infrastructure including homes irrigation systems water supply systems and schools and nearly 100 of the country's electrical grid were destroyed <\s>
<s> on 20 september 1999 the australian-led peacekeeping troops of the international force for east timor interfet deployed to the country and brought the violence to an end <\s>
<s> on 20 may 2002 timor-leste was internationally recognized as an independent state <\s>
<s> in late april 2006 internal tensions threatened the new nation's security when a military strike led to violence and a near breakdown of law and order <\s>
<s> at dili's request an australian-led international stabilization force isf deployed to timor-leste in late may <\s>
<s> in august the un security council established the un integrated mission in timor-leste unmit which included an authorized police presence of over 1,600 personnel <\s>
<s> the isf and unmit restored stability allowing for presidential and parliamentary elections in april and june 2007 in a largely peaceful atmosphere <\s>
<s> in february 2008 a rebel group staged an unsuccessful attack against the president and prime minister <\s>
<s> the ringleader was killed in the attack and the majority of the rebels surrendered in april 2008 <\s>
<s> since the unsuccessful attacks the government has enjoyed one of its longest periods of post-independence stability <\s>
<s> togo french togoland became togo in 1960 <\s>
<s> gnassingbe eyadema installed as military ruler in 1967 ruled togo with a heavy hand for almost four decades <\s>
<s> despite the facade of multiparty elections instituted in the early 1990s the government was largely dominated by president eyadema whose rally of the togolese people rpt party has maintained power almost continually since 1967 and maintains a majority of seats in today's legislature <\s>
<s> upon eyadema's death in february 2005 the military installed the president's son faure gnassingbe and then engineered his formal election two months later <\s>
<s> democratic gains since then allowed togo to hold its first relatively free and fair legislative elections in october 2007 <\s>
<s> after years of political unrest and condemnation from international organizations for human rights abuses togo is finally being re-welcomed into the international community <\s>
<s> tokelau originally settled by polynesian emigrants from surrounding island groups the tokelau islands were made a british protectorate in 1889 <\s>
<s> they were transferred to new zealand administration in 1925 <\s>
<s> referenda held in 2006 and 2007 to change the status of the islands from that of a new zealand territory to one of free association with new zealand did not meet the needed threshold for approval <\s>
<s> suriname first explored by the spaniards in the 16th century and then settled by the english in the mid 17th century suriname became a dutch colony in 1667 <\s>
<s> with the abolition of slavery in 1863 workers were brought in from india and java <\s>
<s> independence from the netherlands was granted in 1975 <\s>
<s> five years later the civilian government was replaced by a military regime that soon declared a socialist republic <\s>
<s> it continued to exert control through a succession of nominally civilian administrations until 1987 when international pressure finally forced a democratic election <\s>
<s> in 1990 the military overthrew the civilian leadership but a democratically elected government a four-party coalition returned to power in 1991 <\s>
<s> the coalition expanded to eight parties in 2005 and has continued to rule since <\s>
<s> svalbard first discovered by the norwegians in the 12th century the islands served as an international whaling base during the 17th and 18th centuries <\s>
<s> norway's sovereignty was recognized in 1920 five years later it officially took over the territory <\s>
<s> swaziland autonomy for the swazis of southern africa was guaranteed by the british in the late 19th century independence was granted in 1968 <\s>
<s> student and labor unrest during the 1990s pressured king mswati iii the world's last absolute monarch to grudgingly allow political reform and greater democracy although he has backslid on these promises in recent years <\s>
<s> a constitution came into effect in 2006 but political parties remain banned <\s>
<s> the african united democratic party tried unsuccessfully to register as an official political party in mid 2006 <\s>
<s> talks over the constitution broke down between the government and progressive groups in 2007 <\s>
<s> swaziland recently surpassed botswana as the country with the world's highest known hiv aids prevalence rate <\s>
<s> sweden a military power during the 17th century sweden has not participated in any war for almost two centuries <\s>
<s> an armed neutrality was preserved in both world wars <\s>
<s> sweden's long-successful economic formula of a capitalist system interlarded with substantial welfare elements was challenged in the 1990s by high unemployment and in 2000-02 and 2009 by the global economic downturns but fiscal discipline over the past several years has allowed the country to weather economic vagaries <\s>
<s> sweden joined the eu in 1995 but the public rejected the introduction of the euro in a 2003 referendum <\s>
<s> switzerland the swiss confederation was founded in 1291 as a defensive alliance among three cantons <\s>
<s> in succeeding years other localities joined the original three <\s>
<s> the swiss confederation secured its independence from the holy roman empire in 1499 <\s>
<s> a constitution of 1848 subsequently modified in 1874 replaced the confederation with a centralized federal government <\s>
<s> switzerland's sovereignty and neutrality have long been honored by the major european powers and the country was not involved in either of the two world wars <\s>
<s> the political and economic integration of europe over the past half century as well as switzerland's role in many un and international organizations has strengthened switzerland's ties with its neighbors <\s>
<s> however the country did not officially become a un member until 2002 <\s>
<s> switzerland remains active in many un and international organizations but retains a strong commitment to neutrality <\s>
<s> syria following world war i france acquired a mandate over the northern portion of the former ottoman empire province of syria <\s>
<s> the french administered the area as syria until granting it independence in 1946 <\s>
<s> the new country lacked political stability however and experienced a series of military coups during its first decades <\s>
<s> syria united with egypt in february 1958 to form the united arab republic <\s>
<s> in september 1961 the two entities separated and the syrian arab republic was reestablished <\s>
<s> in november 1970 hafiz al-asad a member of the socialist ba'th party and the minority alawite sect seized power in a bloodless coup and brought political stability to the country <\s>
<s> in the 1967 arab-israeli war syria lost the golan heights to israel <\s>
<s> during the 1990s syria and israel held occasional peace talks over its return <\s>
<s> following the death of president al-asad his son bashar al-asad was approved as president by popular referendum in july 2000 <\s>
<s> syrian troops stationed in lebanon since 1976 in an ostensible peacekeeping role were withdrawn in april 2005 <\s>
<s> during the july-august 2006 conflict between israel and hizballah syria placed its military forces on alert but did not intervene directly on behalf of its ally hizballah <\s>
<s> in may 2007 bashar al-asad was elected to his second term as president <\s>
<s> taiwan in 1895 military defeat forced china to cede taiwan to japan <\s>
<s> taiwan reverted to chinese control after world war ii <\s>
<s> following the communist victory on the mainland in 1949 2 million nationalists fled to taiwan and established a government using the 1947 constitution drawn up for all of china <\s>
<s> over the next five decades the ruling authorities gradually democratized and incorporated the local population within the governing structure <\s>
<s> in 2000 taiwan underwent its first peaceful transfer of power from the nationalist to the democratic progressive party <\s>
<s> throughout this period the island prospered and became one of east asia's economic tigers <\s>
<s> the dominant political issues continue to be the relationship between taiwan and china specifically the question of taiwan's eventual status as well as domestic political and economic reform <\s>
<s> tajikistan the tajik people came under russian rule in the 1860s and 1870s but russia's hold on central asia weakened following the revolution of 1917 <\s>
<s> bolshevik control of the area was fiercely contested and not fully reestablished until 1925 <\s>
<s> much of present-day sughd province was transferred from the uzbek ssr to the newly formed tajik ssr in 1929 <\s>
<s> ethnic uzbeks form a substantial minority in sughd province <\s>
<s> tajikistan became independent in 1991 following the breakup of the soviet union and experienced a civil war between regional factions from 1992-97 <\s>
<s> there have been no major security incidents in recent years although the country remains the poorest in the former soviet sphere <\s>
<s> attention by the international community since the beginning of the nato intervention in afghanistan has brought increased economic development and security assistance which could create jobs and strengthen stability in the long term <\s>
<s> tajikistan is in the early stages of seeking world trade organization membership and has joined nato's partnership for peace <\s>
<s> tanzania shortly after achieving independence from britain in the early 1960s tanganyika and zanzibar merged to form the nation of tanzania in 1964 <\s>
<s> one-party rule came to an end in 1995 with the first democratic elections held in the country since the 1970s <\s>
<s> zanzibar's semi-autonomous status and popular opposition have led to two contentious elections since 1995 which the ruling party won despite international observers claims of voting irregularities <\s>
<s> thailand a unified thai kingdom was established in the mid 14th century <\s>
<s> known as siam until 1939 thailand is the only southeast asian country never to have been taken over by a european power <\s>
<s> a bloodless revolution in 1932 led to a constitutional monarchy <\s>
<s> in alliance with japan during world war ii thailand became a us treaty ally following the conflict <\s>
<s> a military coup in september 2006 ousted then prime minister thaksin chinnawat <\s>
<s> the interim government held elections in december 2007 that saw the former pro-thaksin people's power party ppp emerge at the head of a coalition government <\s>
<s> the anti-thaksin people's alliance for democracy pad in may 2008 began street demonstrations against the new government eventually occupying the prime minister's office in august and bangkok's two international airports in november <\s>
<s> the pad ended their protests in early december 2008 following a court ruling that dissolved the ruling ppp and two other coalition parties for election violations <\s>
<s> the democrat party then formed a new coalition government and abhisit wetchachiwa became prime minister <\s>
<s> in october 2008 thaksin went into voluntary exile to avoid imprisonment for a corruption conviction and has since agitated his followers from abroad <\s>
<s> thaksin supporters re-organized into the united front for democracy against dictatorship udd and rioted in april 2009 shutting down an asean meeting in phuket and in early 2010 protested a court verdict confiscating most of thaksin's wealth <\s>
<s> between march and may 2010 the udd staged large protests and occupied several blocks of downtown bangkok <\s>
<s> a government operation to disperse the protesters after nine weeks led to clashes that resulted in 89 deaths and an estimated 1.5 billion in arson-related property losses <\s>
<s> these protests exposed major cleavages in the thai body politic which continue to hamper the current government <\s>
<s> since january 2004 thousands have been killed as separatists in thailand's southern ethnic malay-muslim provinces increased the violence associated with their cause <\s>
<s> timor-leste the portuguese began to trade with the island of timor in the early 16th century and colonized it in mid-century <\s>
<s> skirmishing with the dutch in the region eventually resulted in an 1859 treaty in which portugal ceded the western portion of the island <\s>
<s> imperial japan occupied portuguese timor from 1942 to 1945 but portugal resumed colonial authority after the japanese defeat in world war ii <\s>
